           uncertainties in the benchmark experiment.             O0922  1   13

           7 to 2 keV.                                            O0922  1   17

           scattering cross section for boron                     O0922  3    6 
           (D,,G.Dearnaley+,J,PR,108,743,1957) The cross section  O0922  3    7 
           values from that work are about 1.5-2 times those      O0922  3    8 
           reported here and those from other authors.            O0922  3    9 
           (A,C0847002,G.W.Tautfest+,J,PR,103,196,1956)           O0922  3   10 
           (A,,G.D.Symons+,J,NP,46,93,1963)                       O0922  3   11 
           (A,F0322008,R.E.Segel+,J,PR,139,B818,1965)             O0922  3   12 
           (A,O0864003,M.Mayer+,J,NIM/B,143,244,1998)             O0922  3   13 
           In general, our cross section curves agree well in     O0922  3   14 
           shape with the other data, and the absolute values are O0922  3   15 
           in good agreement wiyh those from Symons+ and from     O0922  3   16 
            Segel+. However, some dicrepancies occur: data at 155 O0922  3   17 
           degrees are about 15% higher than those from Tautfest+ O0922  3   18 
           and data at 165 degrees are about 18% higher than the  O0922  3   19 
           ones from Mayer+. It should be noted that these        O0922  3   20 
           discrepancies are essentially systematic, even though  O0922  3   21 
           there is not well-defined trend. - All the comments by O0922  3   22
